URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS483401665	2017-04-15 22:28:01	16556	species	Brown-crested Flycatcher	Myiarchus tyrannulus			1				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Nye	US-NV-023	US-NV_977	33	USFWS_350		Ash Meadows NWR--Bradford Spring	L606033	H	36.4023561	-116.3023424	2017-04-08	11:30:00	obsr684605	S35801307	Incidental	P20	EBIRD				1	0		0	1	1		Stopped because I heard the Yellow Warbler singing and then heard the Myiarchus flycatchers.	Very early arrival date! (Perhaps blown in with the wind that's been blowing steadily from the south for two days.)----I heard an Ash-throated Flycatcher calling 'ka-brick' and their soft rolling 'prrt' call. Before I located the Ash-throated Flycatcher on the west side of the road, I spotted this bird perched on the east side. It was 6 feet off the ground on the outside edge of a mesquite next to the road. Large Myiarchus flycatcher with large heavy bill, rich brown crest and back, light gray throat and chest bib, yellow belly, rufous in wings and tail.  ----I wasn't able to get a photo before it flew. As I worked to find a way into the brush, I could hear its 'Whit' call and a lower burry rolling call than the Ash-throated Flycatcher. The bird kept moving to perches on the back side of bushes and trees from me, staying 6-8 feet off the ground. As I was finally homing in on it, a pair of Ash-throated Flycatchers moved in and chased it off. I was not able to relocate it.----The Ash-throated Flycatchers consistently perched fairly low and often among overhanging branches. Their chest and bellies were much paler, bills shorter, and the birds were more slender than the Brown-crested Flycatcher. The crest and back of the Brown-crested Flycatcher was a warmer and richer brown. The gray of the chest  - darker than on the Ash-throated - and the yellow of the belly - brighter than the pale wash on the Ash-throated - was distinctly separate. The bill was heavier and longer.----Very familiar with both species from southeastern Arizona. We frequently birded in Catalina State Park where we could compare calls and appearance easily.
